## 1. Executive Summary

**FooHut Admin** is the comprehensive administration system for managing every aspect of the FooHut platform. From user management and content moderation to API governance, tokenomics, and support operations â€” this is mission control for the entire ecosystem.

### 1.3 Role Definitions

| Role | Description | Access Level |
|------|-------------|--------------|
| ğŸ”± Super Admin | Founders/C-Suite | Full unrestricted access |
| ğŸ‘‘ Platform Admin | Senior team leads | All user & content management |
| ğŸ’¼ Operations Admin | Support managers | Tickets, billing, account recovery |
| ğŸ›¡ï¸ Security Admin | Security team | Threat monitoring, incident response |
| ğŸ’¬ Chat Moderator | Community moderators | Chat moderation, mute/warn users |
| ğŸ“Š Analyst | Data/Business analysts | Read-only analytics & reports |
| ğŸ« Support Agent | Frontline support | Ticket handling, basic account help |

â”‚  â”‚ â˜ Dismissible    â˜ Link to blog post                                  â”‚â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                        [Schedule]      â”‚â”‚
â”‚  â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜â”‚
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

### 14.2 Email Campaigns

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”

---

## 15. Database Schema

```sql
-- =====================================================
-- FOOHUT ADMIN DATABASE SCHEMA
-- =====================================================

-- Staff / Admin Users
CREATE TABLE admin_users (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'super_admin', 'platform_admin', 'ops_admin', 'security_admin', 'chat_mod', 'support_agent', 'analyst'
  department TEXT,
  title TEXT,
  permissions TEXT DEFAULT '{}', -- JSON override permissions
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  require_2fa BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  ip_whitelist TEXT, -- JSON array of allowed IPs
  created_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_admin_users_role ON admin_users(role);

-- Admin Audit Log
CREATE TABLE admin_audit_log (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  admin_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  action TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'user_ban', 'user_suspend', 'refund', 'config_change', etc.
  target_type TEXT, -- 'user', 'content', 'ticket', 'system', etc.
  target_id TEXT,
  details TEXT, -- JSON with action details
  ip_address TEXT,
  user_agent TEXT,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_audit_admin ON admin_audit_log(admin_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_action ON admin_audit_log(action);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_target ON admin_audit_log(target_type, target_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_created ON admin_audit_log(created_at);

-- User Moderation Actions
CREATE TABLE user_moderation (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  action TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'warning', 'suspend', 'ban', 'delete', 'unsuspend', 'unban'
  reason TEXT NOT NULL,
  reason_code TEXT, -- 'spam', 'harassment', 'tos_violation', etc.
  duration_hours INTEGER, -- NULL for permanent
  internal_notes TEXT,
  admin_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  expires_at DATETIME,
  reverted_at DATETIME,
  reverted_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_moderation_user ON user_moderation(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_moderation_action ON user_moderation(action);

-- Content Reports
CREATE TABLE content_reports (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  content_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'document', 'comment', 'project', 'message', etc.
  content_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  reporter_id TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  report_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'spam', 'harassment', 'copyright', 'inappropriate', etc.
  description TEXT,
  ai_analysis TEXT, -- JSON with AI moderation results
  ai_severity TEXT, -- 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
  ai_confidence REAL,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'reviewing', 'actioned', 'dismissed'
  priority TEXT DEFAULT 'normal', -- 'low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent'
  assigned_to TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  resolution TEXT,
  resolved_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_at DATETIME
);

CREATE INDEX idx_reports_status ON content_reports(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_reports_priority ON content_reports(priority);
CREATE INDEX idx_reports_content ON content_reports(content_type, content_id);

-- Appeals
CREATE TABLE moderation_appeals (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
  moderation_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES user_moderation(id),
  appeal_message TEXT NOT NULL,
  attachments TEXT, -- JSON array of attachment URLs
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', -- 'pending', 'reviewing', 'approved', 'denied'
  ai_recommendation TEXT,
  reviewer_id TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  resolution_notes TEXT,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_at DATETIME
);

CREATE INDEX idx_appeals_status ON moderation_appeals(status);

-- Support Tickets
CREATE TABLE support_tickets (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  ticket_number INTEGER UNIQUE,
  user_id TEXT REFERENCES users(id),
  email TEXT NOT NULL,
  subject TEXT NOT NULL,
  category TEXT, -- 'account', 'billing', 'technical', 'feature_request', 'other'
  priority TEXT DEFAULT 'normal', -- 'low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent'
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'open', -- 'open', 'pending', 'resolved', 'closed'
  source TEXT DEFAULT 'web', -- 'web', 'email', 'chat', 'api'
  assigned_to TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  sla_due_at DATETIME,
  first_response_at DATETIME,
  resolved_at DATETIME,
  csat_score INTEGER, -- 1-5
  csat_feedback TEXT,
  tags TEXT, -- JSON array of tags
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_tickets_status ON support_tickets(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_tickets_assigned ON support_tickets(assigned_to);
CREATE INDEX idx_tickets_user ON support_tickets(user_id);

-- Ticket Messages
CREATE TABLE ticket_messages (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  ticket_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES support_tickets(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_type TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'user', 'agent', 'system'
  sender_id TEXT,
  message TEXT NOT NULL,
  attachments TEXT, -- JSON array
  is_internal BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_ticket_messages ON ticket_messages(ticket_id);

-- Chat Moderation
CREATE TABLE chat_moderation (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
  space_id TEXT,
  action TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'mute', 'timeout', 'warn', 'kick'
  reason TEXT,
  duration_minutes INTEGER,
  message_id TEXT, -- Reference to the offending message
  moderator_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  expires_at DATETIME,
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_chat_mod_user ON chat_moderation(user_id);

-- IP Blocks
CREATE TABLE ip_blocks (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  ip_address TEXT NOT NULL,
  ip_range TEXT, -- CIDR notation for range blocks
  reason TEXT NOT NULL,
  block_type TEXT DEFAULT 'temporary', -- 'temporary', 'permanent'
  expires_at DATETIME,
  blocked_by TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_ip_blocks_ip ON ip_blocks(ip_address);
CREATE INDEX idx_ip_blocks_expires ON ip_blocks(expires_at);

-- Security Incidents
CREATE TABLE security_incidents (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  incident_number TEXT UNIQUE,
  title TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  severity TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'low', 'medium', 'high', 'critical'
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'open', -- 'open', 'investigating', 'mitigating', 'resolved', 'closed'
  affected_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  affected_systems TEXT, -- JSON array
  timeline TEXT, -- JSON array of timeline events
  root_cause TEXT,
  resolution TEXT,
  lessons_learned TEXT,
  lead_responder TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_at DATETIME
);

CREATE INDEX idx_incidents_status ON security_incidents(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_incidents_severity ON security_incidents(severity);

-- Feature Flags
CREATE TABLE feature_flags (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  is_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  rollout_percentage INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  target_segments TEXT, -- JSON array of segment IDs
  config TEXT, -- JSON configuration
  created_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- System Announcements
CREATE TABLE announcements (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  title TEXT NOT NULL,
  message TEXT NOT NULL,
  type TEXT DEFAULT 'info', -- 'info', 'warning', 'alert', 'maintenance'
  display_type TEXT DEFAULT 'banner', -- 'banner', 'modal', 'toast'
  target_audience TEXT DEFAULT 'all', -- 'all', 'pro', 'free', 'custom'
  target_segment TEXT, -- JSON for custom segment
  is_dismissible BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  link_url TEXT,
  link_text TEXT,
  starts_at DATETIME NOT NULL,
  ends_at DATETIME,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
  views INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  dismissals INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_announcements_active ON announcements(is_active, starts_at, ends_at);

-- Email Campaigns
CREATE TABLE email_campaigns (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  name TEXT NOT NULL,
  subject TEXT NOT NULL,
  template_id TEXT,
  content TEXT, -- HTML content
  target_audience TEXT NOT NULL,
  target_count INTEGER,
  status TEXT DEFAULT 'draft', -- 'draft', 'scheduled', 'sending', 'sent', 'failed'
  scheduled_at DATETIME,
  sent_at DATETIME,
  sent_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  opened_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  clicked_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  bounced_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  unsubscribed_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  created_by TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_campaigns_status ON email_campaigns(status);

-- API Key Admin Tracking
CREATE TABLE api_key_admin_actions (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  api_key_id TEXT NOT NULL,
  action TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'created', 'revoked', 'rate_limit_override', 'flagged'
  reason TEXT,
  admin_id TEXT REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Billing Admin Actions
CREATE TABLE billing_admin_actions (
  id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT (uuid()),
  user_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
  action TEXT NOT NULL, -- 'refund', 'credit', 'plan_change', 'invoice_void'
  amount REAL,
  currency TEXT DEFAULT 'USD',
  reason TEXT,
  stripe_refund_id TEXT,
  admin_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES admin_users(id),
  created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_billing_actions_user ON billing_admin_actions(user_id);
```

---

## 16. API Endpoints

### Admin Authentication & Staff

```
POST   /api/v1/admin/auth/login           Admin login (requires 2FA)
POST   /api/v1/admin/auth/logout          Admin logout
GET    /api/v1/admin/auth/me              Current admin info
POST   /api/v1/admin/auth/2fa/verify      Verify 2FA code

GET    /api/v1/admin/staff                List all staff
POST   /api/v1/admin/staff                Add staff member
GET    /api/v1/admin/staff/:id            Get staff details
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/staff/:id            Update staff
DELETE /api/v1/admin/staff/:id            Remove staff
GET    /api/v1/admin/staff/:id/activity   Staff activity log

GET    /api/v1/admin/roles                List roles
POST   /api/v1/admin/roles                Create role
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/roles/:id            Update role permissions
DELETE /api/v1/admin/roles/:id            Delete role
```

### User Management

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/users                List users (with filters)
GET    /api/v1/admin/users/:id            Get user details
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/users/:id            Update user
DELETE /api/v1/admin/users/:id            Delete user

POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/warn       Send warning
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/suspend    Suspend user
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/unsuspend  Unsuspend user
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/ban        Ban user
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/unban      Unban user

GET    /api/v1/admin/users/:id/activity   User activity log
GET    /api/v1/admin/users/:id/sessions   Active sessions
DELETE /api/v1/admin/users/:id/sessions   End all sessions
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/password-reset  Force password reset
POST   /api/v1/admin/users/:id/verify-email    Force verify email

POST   /api/v1/admin/users/bulk           Bulk user action
GET    /api/v1/admin/users/export         Export users
```

### Content Moderation

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/reports              List content reports
GET    /api/v1/admin/reports/:id          Get report details
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/reports/:id          Update report status
POST   /api/v1/admin/reports/:id/action   Take action on report

GET    /api/v1/admin/appeals              List appeals
GET    /api/v1/admin/appeals/:id          Get appeal details
POST   /api/v1/admin/appeals/:id/approve  Approve appeal
POST   /api/v1/admin/appeals/:id/deny     Deny appeal

POST   /api/v1/admin/content/:type/:id/remove    Remove content
POST   /api/v1/admin/content/:type/:id/restore   Restore content
```

### Chat Moderation

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/chat/spaces          List chat spaces
GET    /api/v1/admin/chat/messages        Get messages (with filters)
DELETE /api/v1/admin/chat/messages/:id    Delete message

POST   /api/v1/admin/chat/users/:id/mute      Mute user
POST   /api/v1/admin/chat/users/:id/unmute    Unmute user
POST   /api/v1/admin/chat/users/:id/timeout   Timeout user
POST   /api/v1/admin/chat/users/:id/warn      Warn user

GET    /api/v1/admin/chat/automod         Auto-mod settings
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/chat/automod         Update auto-mod settings
```

### Support

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/tickets              List tickets
POST   /api/v1/admin/tickets              Create ticket
GET    /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id          Get ticket
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id          Update ticket
POST   /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id/assign   Assign ticket
POST   /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id/reply    Reply to ticket
POST   /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id/close    Close ticket
POST   /api/v1/admin/tickets/:id/escalate Escalate ticket

GET    /api/v1/admin/emails               List support emails
POST   /api/v1/admin/emails/:id/ticket    Create ticket from email
POST   /api/v1/admin/emails/:id/reply     Reply to email
POST   /api/v1/admin/emails/:id/archive   Archive email

GET    /api/v1/admin/templates            List response templates
POST   /api/v1/admin/templates            Create template
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/templates/:id        Update template
DELETE /api/v1/admin/templates/:id        Delete template
```

### API Management

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/api/stats            API statistics
GET    /api/v1/admin/api/endpoints        List endpoints
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/api/endpoints/:id    Update endpoint config

GET    /api/v1/admin/api/keys             List API keys
GET    /api/v1/admin/api/keys/:id         Get key details
POST   /api/v1/admin/api/keys/:id/revoke  Revoke key
POST   /api/v1/admin/api/keys/:id/flag    Flag suspicious key

GET    /api/v1/admin/api/rate-limits      Get rate limit config
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/api/rate-limits      Update rate limits
POST   /api/v1/admin/api/rate-limits/override  Add rate limit override
DELETE /api/v1/admin/api/rate-limits/override/:id  Remove override
```

### Billing & Tokenomics

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/billing/stats        Billing statistics
GET    /api/v1/admin/billing/plans        List plans
POST   /api/v1/admin/billing/plans        Create plan
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/billing/plans/:id    Update plan

GET    /api/v1/admin/billing/users/:id    User billing info
POST   /api/v1/admin/billing/users/:id/refund     Issue refund
POST   /api/v1/admin/billing/users/:id/credit     Add credits
POST   /api/v1/admin/billing/users/:id/plan       Change plan
POST   /api/v1/admin/billing/users/:id/coupon     Apply coupon

GET    /api/v1/admin/credits/stats        Credit statistics
GET    /api/v1/admin/credits/packages     List credit packages
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/credits/packages/:id Update package
```

### Database

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/database/stats       Database statistics
GET    /api/v1/admin/database/tables      List tables
POST   /api/v1/admin/database/query       Execute query (read-only)
GET    /api/v1/admin/database/backups     List backups
POST   /api/v1/admin/database/backups     Create backup
POST   /api/v1/admin/database/restore     Restore from backup
```

### Security

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/security/dashboard   Security dashboard
GET    /api/v1/admin/security/events      Security events
GET    /api/v1/admin/security/threats     Active threats

GET    /api/v1/admin/security/ip-blocks   List blocked IPs
POST   /api/v1/admin/security/ip-blocks   Block IP
DELETE /api/v1/admin/security/ip-blocks/:id  Unblock IP

GET    /api/v1/admin/security/incidents   List incidents
POST   /api/v1/admin/security/incidents   Create incident
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/security/incidents/:id  Update incident
POST   /api/v1/admin/security/incidents/:id/resolve  Resolve incident
```

### System & Configuration

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/config               Get system config
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/config               Update config

GET    /api/v1/admin/feature-flags        List feature flags
POST   /api/v1/admin/feature-flags        Create flag
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/feature-flags/:id    Update flag
DELETE /api/v1/admin/feature-flags/:id    Delete flag

GET    /api/v1/admin/announcements        List announcements
POST   /api/v1/admin/announcements        Create announcement
PATCH  /api/v1/admin/announcements/:id    Update announcement
DELETE /api/v1/admin/announcements/:id    Delete announcement

GET    /api/v1/admin/audit-log            Get audit log
GET    /api/v1/admin/audit-log/export     Export audit log
```

### Analytics & Reports

```
GET    /api/v1/admin/analytics/dashboard  Analytics dashboard
GET    /api/v1/admin/analytics/users      User analytics
GET    /api/v1/admin/analytics/revenue    Revenue analytics
GET    /api/v1/admin/analytics/api        API analytics
GET    /api/v1/admin/analytics/support    Support analytics

GET    /api/v1/admin/reports              List report templates
POST   /api/v1/admin/reports/generate     Generate report
GET    /api/v1/admin/reports/scheduled    List scheduled reports
POST   /api/v1/admin/reports/scheduled    Create scheduled report
```

---

## 18. Implementation Roadmap

### Phase 1: Core Admin (Weeks 1-3)
- [ ] Admin authentication & 2FA
- [ ] Staff management & roles
- [ ] Basic user management
- [ ] Audit logging

### Phase 2: User & Content Moderation (Weeks 4-6)
- [ ] Full user profile view
- [ ] Moderation actions (warn, suspend, ban)
- [ ] Content report queue
- [ ] Appeals management

### Phase 3: Support Center (Weeks 7-9)
- [ ] Ticket system
- [ ] Email inbox integration
- [ ] Response templates
- [ ] SLA tracking

### Phase 4: Chat Moderation (Weeks 10-11)
- [ ] Live chat monitor
- [ ] Auto-moderation
- [ ] Word filters
- [ ] Mute/timeout system

### Phase 5: API & Billing (Weeks 12-14)
- [ ] API dashboard
- [ ] Rate limit management
- [ ] API key administration
- [ ] Billing management
- [ ] Refund processing

### Phase 6: Database & Security (Weeks 15-17)
- [ ] Database explorer
- [ ] Backup management
- [ ] Security dashboard
- [ ] Incident management
- [ ] IP blocking

### Phase 7: Analytics & Communications (Weeks 18-20)
- [ ] Analytics dashboard
- [ ] Report generation
- [ ] Announcements
- [ ] Email campaigns
- [ ] Feature flags

---

## 19. Success Metrics

| Metric | Target | Measurement |
|--------|--------|-------------|
| Ticket response time | <2 hours | Average first response |
| Ticket resolution | <24 hours | Average resolution time |
| CSAT score | >4.5/5 | Customer satisfaction |
| Moderation queue | <1 hour | Time to review |
| Appeal processing | <48 hours | Time to decision |
| Staff audit coverage | 100% | All actions logged |
| System uptime | 99.99% | Admin portal availability |
